CREATE TABLE dealer(dealer_ID INTEGER NOT NULL,	address VARCHAR(100) NULL, phone CHAR(12) NULL, PRIMARY KEY (dealer_ID));
CREATE TABLE customer(customer_ID INTEGER NOT NULL,type VARCHAR(11) NOT NULL CHECK (type IN ('private', 'enterprise')),name VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL,address VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,phone CHAR(12) NULL, gender VARCHAR(8) NULL CHECK (gender IN ('male', 'female', 'company')), income INTEGER NULL, PRIMARY KEY (customer_ID));
CREATE TABLE company(company_name VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL, PRIMARY KEY (company_name));
CREATE TABLE brand(brand_name VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL, company_name VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL, PRIMARY KEY (brand_name), FOREIGN KEY (company_name) REFERENCES company(company_name));
CREATE TABLE model(model_ID INTEGER NOT NULL, brand_name VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL, model_type VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL, model_name VARCHAR(50) NULL, model_year YEAR NOT NULL, is_aval boolean NOT NULL, PRIMARY KEY (model_ID), FOREIGN KEY (brand_name) REFERENCES brand(brand_name));
CREATE TABLE car_option(option_ID CHAR(21) NOT NULL, paint VARCHAR(25) NOT NULL, wheels VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL, interior VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL, seat INTEGER NOT NULL, self_driving boolean NULL, PRIMARY KEY (option_ID));
CREATE TABLE option_aval(model_ID INTEGER NOT NULL, option_ID CHAR(21) NOT NULL, PRIMARY KEY (model_ID,option_ID), FOREIGN KEY (model_ID) REFERENCES model(model_ID), FOREIGN KEY (option_ID) REFERENCES car_option(option_ID));
CREATE TABLE vehicle(VIN INTEGER NOT NULL, model_ID INTEGER NOT NULL, option_ID CHAR(21) NOT NULL,customer_ID INTEGER NULL, PRIMARY KEY (VIN), FOREIGN KEY (customer_ID) REFERENCES customer(customer_ID), FOREIGN KEY (model_ID,option_ID) REFERENCES option_aval(model_ID,option_ID));
CREATE TABLE sells_vehicle(VIN INTEGER NOT NULL,dealer_ID INTEGER NOT NULL,date DATE NULL,price INTEGER NULL, PRIMARY KEY (VIN), FOREIGN KEY (dealer_ID) REFERENCES dealer(dealer_ID),	FOREIGN KEY (VIN) REFERENCES vehicle(VIN));
CREATE TABLE supplier(supplier_name VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL, PRIMARY KEY (supplier_name));
CREATE TABLE part(part_ID INTEGER NOT NULL, part_type VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL, PRIMARY KEY (part_ID));
CREATE TABLE supply_plant(plant_name VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL,company_name VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL, PRIMARY KEY (plant_name), FOREIGN KEY (company_name) REFERENCES company(company_name));
CREATE TABLE sup_makes_part(part_ID INTEGER NOT NULL,supplier_name VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL,date DATE NULL,PRIMARY KEY (part_ID), FOREIGN KEY (supplier_name) REFERENCES supplier(supplier_name),FOREIGN KEY (part_ID) REFERENCES part(part_ID));
CREATE TABLE pnt_makes_part(plant_name VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL, part_ID INTEGER NOT NULL, date DATE NULL, PRIMARY KEY (part_ID), FOREIGN KEY (plant_name) REFERENCES supply_plant(plant_name), FOREIGN KEY (part_ID) REFERENCES part(part_ID));
CREATE TABLE assembly_plant(plant_name VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL, company_name VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL, PRIMARY KEY (plant_name), FOREIGN KEY (company_name) REFERENCES company(company_name));
CREATE TABLE makes_vehicle(VIN INTEGER NOT NULL, plant_name VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL, date DATE NULL, PRIMARY KEY (VIN), FOREIGN KEY (plant_name) REFERENCES assembly_plant(plant_name), FOREIGN KEY (VIN) REFERENCES vehicle(VIN));
CREATE TABLE uses_part (part_ID INTEGER NOT NULL, VIN INTEGER NOT NULL, PRIMARY KEY (part_ID), FOREIGN KEY (part_ID) REFERENCES part(part_ID), FOREIGN KEY (VIN) REFERENCES vehicle(VIN));
